"""Multi-axis RoPE pre-attention prep — Triton v3 (SM120 Blackwell).

Two kernel types:
- Large shapes: Grid=(B*T, 1), each program loops over all H heads (serial).
- Small H shapes: Grid=(B*T*H, 1), each program processes exactly one (b,h,t).

The second gives more parallel SMs for better occupancy with small head counts.
"""

import torch
import triton
import triton.language as tl
import torch.nn as nn


@triton.jit
def _rope_serial_h_kernel(
    x_ptr, x_out_ptr,
    cos_cache_ptr, sin_cache_ptr,
    pos_t_ptr, pos_h_ptr, pos_w_ptr,
    B_val: tl.constexpr, T_val: tl.constexpr,
    H_val: tl.constexpr, D_val: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xb, stride_xt, stride_xh, stride_xd,
    stride_ob, stride_oh, stride_ot, stride_od,
    s0: tl.constexpr, s1: tl.constexpr,
    half: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Grid=(B*T). Serial loop over H heads."""
    pid_bt = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_b = pid_bt // T_val
    pid_t = pid_bt % T_val

    pos_idx = pid_b * T_val + pid_t
    p_t = tl.load(pos_t_ptr + pos_idx)
    p_h = tl.load(pos_h_ptr + pos_idx)
    p_w = tl.load(pos_w_ptr + pos_idx)

    d_offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
    mask = d_offs < D_val

    cos_t = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sin_t = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    cos_h = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sin_h = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    cos_w = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sin_w = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)

    axis_idx = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs, d_offs - half)
    is_t = axis_idx < s0
    is_h = (axis_idx >= s0) & (axis_idx < s0 + s1)
    cos_v = tl.where(is_t, cos_t, tl.where(is_h, cos_h, cos_w))
    sin_v = tl.where(is_t, sin_t, tl.where(is_h, sin_h, sin_w))

    perm = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs + half, d_offs - half)
    sign = tl.where(d_offs < half, -1.0, 1.0)

    for h in tl.static_range(H_val):
        x_base = pid_b * stride_xb + pid_t * stride_xt + h * stride_xh
        x  = tl.load(x_ptr  + x_base + d_offs * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        xr = tl.load(x_ptr + x_base + perm  * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        xr = xr * sign
        out = x * cos_v + xr * sin_v
        o_base = pid_b * stride_ob + h * stride_oh + pid_t * stride_ot
        tl.store(x_out_ptr + o_base + d_offs * stride_od, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)


@triton.jit
def _rope_parallel_h_kernel(
    x_ptr, x_out_ptr,
    cos_cache_ptr, sin_cache_ptr,
    pos_t_ptr, pos_h_ptr, pos_w_ptr,
    B_val: tl.constexpr, T_val: tl.constexpr,
    D_val: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xb, stride_xt, stride_xh, stride_xd,
    stride_ob, stride_oh, stride_ot, stride_od,
    s0: tl.constexpr, s1: tl.constexpr,
    half: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Grid=(B*T*H). Each program = exactly one (b,h,t)."""
    pid_bth = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_b = pid_bth // tl.num_programs(1)
    pid_th = pid_bth % tl.num_programs(1)
    # Actually this doesn't work cleanly. Let me pass explicit B, T, H.
    pass


@triton.jit
def _rope_flat_kernel(
    x_ptr, x_out_ptr,
    cos_cache_ptr, sin_cache_ptr,
    pos_t_ptr, pos_h_ptr, pos_w_ptr,
    H_val: tl.constexpr, D_val: tl.constexpr,
    total_bt: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xb, stride_xt, stride_xh, stride_xd,
    stride_ob, stride_oh, stride_ot, stride_od,
    s0: tl.constexpr, s1: tl.constexpr,
    half: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Grid=(B*T*H). Each program = one (b,h,t). No serial loop."""
    pid = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_h = pid % H_val
    pid_bt = pid // H_val
    pid_b = pid_bt // (total_bt // H_val)  # total_bt = B*T, so pid_bt // (BT/H) doesn't work
    # This approach is getting messy. Let me just pass B and T directly.
    pass


@triton.jit
def _rope_one_per_head(
    x_ptr, x_out_ptr,
    cos_cache_ptr, sin_cache_ptr,
    pos_t_ptr, pos_h_ptr, pos_w_ptr,
    B_val: tl.constexpr, T_val: tl.constexpr,
    H_val: tl.constexpr, D_val: tl.constexpr,
    stride_xb, stride_xt, stride_xh, stride_xd,
    stride_ob, stride_oh, stride_ot, stride_od,
    s0: tl.constexpr, s1: tl.constexpr,
    half: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Grid=(B*T*H). Each program = exactly one (b, h, t).
    Cache cos/sin per (b,t), but no head loop - maximum parallelism."""
    pid = tl.program_id(0)
    total_bt = B_val * T_val
    pid_h = pid % H_val
    pid_bth = pid // H_val
    pid_b = pid_bth // T_val
    pid_t = pid_bth % T_val

    pos_idx = pid_b * T_val + pid_t
    p_t = tl.load(pos_t_ptr + pos_idx)
    p_h = tl.load(pos_h_ptr + pos_idx)
    p_w = tl.load(pos_w_ptr + pos_idx)

    d_offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
    mask = d_offs < D_val

    cos_t = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sin_t = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    cos_h = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sin_h = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    cos_w = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sin_w = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)

    axis_idx = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs, d_offs - half)
    is_t = axis_idx < s0
    is_h = (axis_idx >= s0) & (axis_idx < s0 + s1)
    cos_v = tl.where(is_t, cos_t, tl.where(is_h, cos_h, cos_w))
    sin_v = tl.where(is_t, sin_t, tl.where(is_h, sin_h, sin_w))

    perm = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs + half, d_offs - half)
    sign = tl.where(d_offs < half, -1.0, 1.0)

    x_base = pid_b * stride_xb + pid_t * stride_xt + pid_h * stride_xh
    x  = tl.load(x_ptr  + x_base + d_offs * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    xr = tl.load(x_ptr + x_base + perm * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    xr = xr * sign
    out = x * cos_v + xr * sin_v
    o_base = pid_b * stride_ob + pid_h * stride_oh + pid_t * stride_ot
    tl.store(x_out_ptr + o_base + d_offs * stride_od, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)


class Model(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, B, T, Hq, Hkv, D, mrope_section, max_pos):
        super().__init__()
        assert sum(mrope_section) == D // 2
        self.B, self.T = B, T
        self.Hq, self.Hkv, self.D = Hq, Hkv, D
        self.mrope_section = tuple(mrope_section)
        self.max_pos = max_pos

        inv_freq = _build_inv_freq(D)
        pos = torch.arange(max_pos, dtype=torch.float32)
        freqs = torch.outer(pos, inv_freq)
        emb = torch.cat([freqs, freqs], dim=-1)
        self.register_buffer("cos_cache", emb.cos().to(torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("sin_cache", emb.sin().to(torch.bfloat16))

    def _next_pow2(self, n):
        v = 1
        while v < n:
            v *= 2
        return v

    def _launch(self, x, x_out, H, method):
        B, T, _, D = x.shape
        s0, s1, _ = self.mrope_section
        half = D // 2
        BLOCK_D = self._next_pow2(D)

        if method == "parallel":
            grid = (B * T * H,)
            _rope_one_per_head[grid](
                x, x_out,
                self.cos_cache, self.sin_cache,
                x.reshape(-1, 1, 1)[:, 0, 0].data_ptr(),  # wrong
                pos_h, pos_w,
                B_val=B, T_val=T, H_val=H, D_val=D,
                stride_xb=T*H*D, stride_xt=H*D, stride_xh=D, stride_xd=1,
                stride_ob=H*T*D, stride_oh=T*D, stride_ot=D, stride_od=1,
                s0=s0, s1=s1, half=half, BLOCK_D=BLOCK_D,
                num_warps=1,
            )
        else:
            grid = (B * T,)
            _rope_serial_h_kernel[grid](
                x, x_out,
                self.cos_cache, self.sin_cache,
                x.reshape(-1, 1, 1)[:, 0, 0].data_ptr(),  # wrong
                pos_h, pos_w,
                B_val=B, T_val=T, H_val=H, D_val=D,
                stride_xb=T*H*D, stride_xt=H*D, stride_xh=D, stride_xd=1,
                stride_ob=H*T*D, stride_oh=T*D, stride_ot=D, stride_od=1,
                s0=s0, s1=s1, half=half, BLOCK_D=BLOCK_D,
                num_warps=1, num_stages=4,
            )

    def forward(self, q, k, pos_t, pos_h, pos_w):
        B, T, Hq, D = q.shape
        _, _, Hkv, _ = k.shape
        s0, s1, _ = self.mrope_section

        q_out = torch.empty(B, Hq, T, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=q.device)
        k_out = torch.empty(B, Hkv, T, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=k.device)

        BLOCK_D = self._next_pow2(D)
        half = D // 2

        _rope_serial_h_kernel[(B * T,)](
            q, q_out,
            self.cos_cache, self.sin_cache,
            pos_t, pos_h, pos_w,
            B_val=B, T_val=T, H_val=Hq, D_val=D,
            stride_xb=T*Hq*D, stride_xt=Hq*D, stride_xh=D, stride_xd=1,
            stride_ob=Hq*T*D, stride_oh=T*D, stride_ot=D, stride_od=1,
            s0=s0, s1=s1, half=half, BLOCK_D=BLOCK_D,
            num_warps=1, num_stages=4,
        )
        _rope_serial_h_kernel[(B * T,)](
            k, k_out,
            self.cos_cache, self.sin_cache,
            pos_t, pos_h, pos_w,
            B_val=B, T_val=T, H_val=Hkv, D_val=D,
            stride_xb=T*Hkv*D, stride_xt=Hkv*D, stride_xh=D, stride_xd=1,
            stride_ob=Hkv*T*D, stride_oh=T*D, stride_ot=D, stride_od=1,
            s0=s0, s1=s1, half=half, BLOCK_D=BLOCK_D,
            num_warps=1, num_stages=4,
        )

        return q_out, k_out


def _build_inv_freq(D, base=10000.0):
    return 1.0 / (base ** (torch.arange(0, D, 2, dtype=torch.float32) / D))
OK, this is about the same as the separate Q+K version (52.6% vs 51.0%). The fusion doesn't help because each program still has to loop through Q+K heads sequentially. The benefit would be avoiding the second kernel launch overhead, but that's negligible compared to the memory bandwidth. Let me try a fundamentally different approach: since Triton 3.6.0 is available, let me use its newer features like `triton.language.core.load/store` with pointer vectors or batched loads. Actually, the key insight I'm missing: I should try increasing the grid size to get more SMs saturated, especially for shape 2. Let me try a kernel where I parallelize both T and H dimensions, effectively having grid = (B, T, H):

1: """Canonical shape sweep for multi-axis RoPE pre-attention.
2: 
3: Sized for Qwen2-VL-style vision-language inference: long T, GQA, mrope_section
4: splitting D/2 across temporal/height/width axes. Mix of base, long-context,
5: small-head-dim, and very-long-context.
6: """
7: 
8: SHAPES = [
9:     # Qwen2-VL base: T=4k, head_dim=128, GQA 32:8, mrope [16,24,24]
10:     {"B": 1, "T": 4096,  "Hq": 32, "Hkv": 8, "D": 128,
11:      "mrope_section": (16, 24, 24), "max_pos": 32768},
12: 
13:     # Qwen2-VL 7B-style long context, narrower kv heads

5: 
6: # FLOPs per call: rotate-half on q and k.
7: # Per element: out = a*cos + b*sin -> 3 flops/elem (1 mul + 1 mul + 1 add).

+++ b//home/infatoshi/cuda/KernelBench-Hard/problems/09_fmha_preattn_mrope/solution.py
@@ -0,0 +1,235 @@
+"""Optimized multi-axis RoPE pre-attention prep using Triton (SM120).
+
+Fused kernel: gather per-axis cos/sin from cache, mix by mrope_section,
+apply rotate-half rotation, transpose (B,T,H,D)->(B,H,T,D) in one pass.
+"""
+
+import torch
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+import torch.nn as nn
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _rope_fwd_kernel(
+    x_ptr,
+    x_out_ptr,
+    pos_t_ptr,
+    pos_h_ptr,
+    pos_w_ptr,
+    cos_cache_ptr,
+    sin_cache_ptr,
+    B_val: tl.constexpr,
+    T_val: tl.constexpr,
+    H_val: tl.constexpr,
+    D_val: tl.constexpr,
+    stride_xb,
+    stride_xt,
+    stride_xh,
+    stride_xd,
+    stride_ob,
+    stride_oh,
+    stride_ot,
+    stride_od,
+    stride_pos_b,
+    stride_pos_t,
+    s0: tl.constexpr,
+    s1: tl.constexpr,
+    half: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Each program handles one (b, h, t). Loads full D, rotates, writes to (B,H,T,D)."""
+    pid_bh = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_t = tl.program_id(1)
+
+    # Decode (batch, head)
+    pid_b = pid_bh // H_val
+    pid_h = pid_bh % H_val
+
+    # Position index in (B,T) array
+    pos_idx = pid_b * stride_pos_b + pid_t * stride_pos_t
+
+    # Load position IDs
+    p_t = tl.load(pos_t_ptr + pos_idx)
+    p_h = tl.load(pos_h_ptr + pos_idx)
+    p_w = tl.load(pos_w_ptr + pos_idx)
+
+    # Dimension offsets
+    d_offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
+    mask = d_offs < D_val
+    half_mask = d_offs < half
+
+    # Base offset into input tensor (B,T,H,D)
+    x_base = pid_b * stride_xb + pid_t * stride_xt + pid_h * stride_xh
+
+    # Output base offset (B,H,T,D)
+    o_base = pid_b * stride_ob + pid_h * stride_oh + pid_t * stride_ot
+
+    # Load x vector
+    x = tl.load(x_ptr + x_base + d_offs * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+
+    # Load cos/sin for temporal axis
+    cos_t_ = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+    sin_t_ = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+
+    # Load cos/sin for height axis
+    cos_h_ = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+    sin_h_ = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+
+    # Load cos/sin for width axis
+    cos_w_ = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+    sin_w_ = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+
+    # Mix axes: for d in [0, half), axis_idx = d; for d in [half, D), axis_idx = d - half
+    axis_idx = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs, d_offs - half)
+
+    # Axis assignment masks
+    is_temporal = axis_idx < s0
+    is_height = (axis_idx >= s0) & (axis_idx < s0 + s1)
+    # is_width is implicit (the rest)
+
+    # Select cos/sin per axis
+    cos = tl.where(is_temporal, cos_t_, tl.where(is_height, cos_h_, cos_w_))
+    sin = tl.where(is_temporal, sin_t_, tl.where(is_height, sin_h_, sin_w_))
+
+    # rotate_half(x) = [-x[half:], x[:half]]
+    # For d < half: x_rot[d] = -x[d + half]
+    # For d >= half: x_rot[d] = x[d - half]
+    # Permute offsets
+    permuted_offs = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs + half, d_offs - half)
+    x_rot_loaded = tl.load(x_ptr + x_base + permuted_offs * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0)
+    x_rot_loaded = tl.where(d_offs < half, -x_rot_loaded, x_rot_loaded)
+
+    # Apply rotation: out = x*cos + x_rot*sin
+    x_fp32 = x.to(tl.float32)
+    cos_fp32 = cos.to(tl.float32)
+    sin_fp32 = sin.to(tl.float32)
+    x_rot_fp32 = x_rot_loaded.to(tl.float32)
+
+    out = (x_fp32 * cos_fp32) + (x_rot_fp32 * sin_fp32)
+    out = out.to(tl.bfloat16)
+
+    # Store in transposed layout (B,H,T,D)
+    tl.store(x_out_ptr + o_base + d_offs * stride_od, out, mask=mask)
+
+
+class Model(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(self, B: int, T: int, Hq: int, Hkv: int, D: int,
+                 mrope_section: tuple[int, int, int], max_pos: int):
+        super().__init__()
+        assert sum(mrope_section) == D // 2, \
+            f"mrope_section must sum to D/2, got {mrope_section} sum={sum(mrope_section)} D/2={D//2}"
+        self.B, self.T = B, T
+        self.Hq, self.Hkv, self.D = D
+        self.mrope_section = tuple(mrope_section)
+        self.max_pos = max_pos
+
+        inv_freq = _build_inv_freq(D)
+        pos = torch.arange(max_pos, dtype=torch.float32)
+        freqs = torch.outer(pos, inv_freq)
+        emb = torch.cat([freqs, freqs], dim=-1)
+        self.register_buffer("cos_cache", emb.cos().to(torch.bfloat16))
+        self.register_buffer("sin_cache", emb.sin().to(torch.bfloat16))
+
+        # Precompute grid and strides
+        self._q_grid = (B * Hq, T)
+        self._k_grid = (B * Hkv, T)
+        self._block_d = self._next_pow2(D)
+
+        q_strides = self._strides(B, T, Hq, D)
+        k_strides = self._strides(B, T, Hkv, D)
+        self._q_strides = q_strides
+        self._k_strides = k_strides
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def _strides(B, T, H, D):
+        return {
+            'stride_xb': T * H * D,
+            'stride_xt': H * D,
+            'stride_xh': D,
+            'stride_xd': 1,
+            'stride_ob': H * T * D,
+            'stride_oh': T * D,
+            'stride_ot': D,
+            'stride_od': 1,
+        }
+
+    @staticmethod
+    def _next_pow2(n):
+        v = 1
+        while v < n:
+            v *= 2
+        return v
+
+    def forward(
+        self,
+        q: torch.Tensor, k: torch.Tensor,
+        pos_t: torch.Tensor, pos_h: torch.Tensor, pos_w: torch.Tensor,
+    ) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
+        B, T, Hq, D = q.shape
+        _, _, Hkv, _ = k.shape
+        s0, s1, _ = self.mrope_section
+        half = D // 2
+        BLOCK_D = self._next_pow2(D)
+
+        # Allocate outputs in (B,H,T,D) layout
+        q_out = torch.empty(B, Hq, T, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=q.device)
+        k_out = torch.empty(B, Hkv, T, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=k.dev

... (1531 more chars)

Run the benchmark script and also profile the solution to understand the bottleneck. 

First, change to: /home/infatoshi/cuda/KernelBench-Hard/problems/09_fmha_preattn_mrope

```python
import torch
import torch.profiler
import sys
sys.path.insert(0, '/home/infatoshi/cuda/KernelBench-Hard')

# Import solution
import solution

B, T, Hq, Hkv, D = 1, 4096, 32, 8, 128
MAX_POS = 32768
MROPE_SECTION = (16, 24, 24)

dev = "cuda:0"
model = solution.Model(B, T, Hq, Hkv, D, MROPE_SECTION, MAX_POS).to(dev).eval()

q = torch.randn(B, T, Hq, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=dev) * 0.5
k = torch.randn(B, T, Hkv, D, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=dev) * 0.5
pos_t = torch.randint(0, MAX_POS, (B, T), dtype=torch.int64, device=dev)
pos_h = torch.randint(0, MAX_POS, (B, T), dtype=torch.int64, device=dev)
pos_w = torch.randint(0, MAX_POS, (B, T), dtype=torch.int64, device=dev)

# Warmup 
with torch.no_grad():
    model(q, k, pos_t, pos_h, pos_w)
    
torch.cuda.synchronize()

# Time with profiler
prof = torch.profiler.profile(
    activities=[torch.profiler.ProfilerActivity.CUDA],
    record_shapes=True,
)
for _ in range(50):
    with torch.no_grad():
        model(q, k, pos_t, pos_h, pos_w)
torch.cuda.synchronize()

prof.stop()
print(prof.key_averages().table(sort_by="self_cuda_time_total", row_limit=20))
```

+"""Optimized multi-axis RoPE pre-attention prep using Triton (SM120 Blackwell).

+This maximizes L2 cache reuse on the cos/sin cache lookups since all heads
+in a block share the same position IDs.
+
+Per-axis mixing follows mRoPE convention:
+- First s0 pair-indices [0..s0) use temporal axis
+- Next s1 [s0..s0+s1) use height axis  
+- Remaining [s0+s1..D/2) use width axis
+- Second half [D/2..D) mirrors: index d gets axis d - D/2
 """

+"""Hand-tuned CUDA C++ kernel for multi-axis RoPE pre-attention prep (SM120 Blackwell).
+
+Single fused kernel: one thread per (b, t, h, D/2) pair, loads two bf16 at once,
+does both elements in the pair, computes cos/sin from the same axis lookup,
+applies rotate-half in one pass, and writes transposed (B,H,T,D).
+
+Uses __ldg for read-only loads and vectorized bf16x2 stores.
+"""
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline
+import os
+import tempfile
+
+CUDA_SRC = r"""
+#include <cuda_fp16.h>
+#include <cuda_bf16.h>
+#include <cooperative_groups.h>
+
+namespace cg = cooperative_groups;
+
+// BF16 -> float2
+static __device__ __forceinline__ float2 bf16x2_to_float2(
+    __nv_bfloat162 v) {
+  return __bfloat1622float2(v);
+}
+
+static __device__ __forceinline__ __nv_bfloat162 float2_to_bf16x2(
+    float x, float y) {
+  return __floats2bfloat162_rn(x, y);
+}
+
+template <const int D>
+__global__ void __launch_bounds__(256) mrope_kernel(
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ x_in,     // (B, T, Hx, D)
+    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ x_out,          // (B, Hx, T, D)
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_t,
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_h,
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_w,
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ cos_cache, // (max_pos, D)
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ sin_cache,
+    const int B,
+    const int T,
+    const int Hx,
+    const int s0,
+    const int s1
+) {
+    // Each block of threads handles one (b, t); threads distribute over heads.
+    // Each thread handles ALL elements of D for ONE head.
+    // Grid = (B * T, Hx), block = (num_threads), each thread processes D elements.
+
+    const int bt = blockIdx.x;  // (B * T)
+    const int b = bt / T;
+    const int t = bt % T;
+
+    // Position IDs (shared across all threads in block)
+    const int pos_off = b * T + t;
+    const int64_t pt = __ldg(pos_t + pos_off);
+    const int64_t ph = __ldg(pos_h + pos_off);
+    const int64_t pw = __ldg(pos_w + pos_off);
+
+    // Thread handles multiple heads (if num_heads > block_size)
+    const int h = blockIdx.y * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
+    if (h >= Hx) return;
+
+    constexpr int half = D / 2;
+    constexpr int d_pairs = D / 2;  // number of bf16x2 pairs
+    
+    // Load cos/sin cache for each pair
+    __nv_bfloat162 cos_d[D/2];
+    __nv_bfloat162 sin_d[D/2];
+    
+    #pragma unroll
+    for (int p = 0; p < D/2; p++) {
+        int di = p;
+        int axis = (di < half) ? di : (di - half);
+        
+        const __nv_bfloat162 *cache_cos_row, *cache_sin_row;
+        if (axis < s0) {
+            cache_cos_row = (const __nv_bfloat162*)&cos_cache[pt * D];
+            cache_sin_row = (const __nv_bfloat162*)&sin_cache[pt * D];
+        } else if (axis < s0 + s1) {
+            cache_cos_row = (const __nv_bfloat162*)&cos_cache[ph * D];
+            cache_sin_row = (const __nv_bfloat162*)&sin_cache[ph * D];
+        } else {
+            cache_cos_row = (const __nv_bfloat162*)&cos_cache[pw * D];
+            cache_sin_row = (const __nv_bfloat162*)&sin_cache[pw * D];
+        }
+        cos_d[p] = __ldg(&cache_cos_row[p]);
+        sin_d[p] = __ldg(&cache_sin_row[p]);
+    }
+
+    // Input stride: BxTxDxH
+    const long long x_base = (long long)b * T * Hx * D + (long long)t * Hx * D + (long long)h * D;
+    const __nv_bfloat162* x_in_vec = (const __nv_bfloat162*)&x_in[x_base];
+    
+    for (int p = 0; p < d_pairs; p++) {
+        // Load x[p] - this is one pair at offset p
+        __nv_bfloat162 x_p = __ldg(&x_in_vec[p]);
+        
+        // rotate_half for pair p:
+        // if p < half/2 (i.e., both elements in first half): rot[p] = -x[p + half/2]
+        // if p >= half/2: rot[p] = x[p - half/2]
+        
+        __nv_bfloat162 rot_p;
+        float2 x_f0 = __bfloat1622float2(x_p);
+        int mirror_p = (p < half/2) ? (p + half/2) : (p - half/2);
+        
+        __nv_bfloat162 x_mirror = __ldg(&x_in_vec[mirror_p]);
+        float2 xm_f = __bfloat1622float2(x_mirror);
+        
+        if (p < half/2) {
+            // negate
+            xm_f.x = -xm_f.x;
+            xm_f.y = -xm_f.y;
+        }
+        rot_p = __floats2bfloat162_rn(xm_f.x, xm_f.y);
+
+        // Apply: out = x * cos + rot * sin  
+        float2 cos_f = __bfloat1622float2(cos_d[p]);
+        float2 sin_f = __bfloat1622float2(sin_d[p]);
+        
+        float2 out_f;
+        out_f.x = x_f0.x * cos_f.x + xm_f.x * sin_f.x;
+        out_f.y = x_f0.y * cos_f.y + xm_f.y * sin_f.y;
+        
+        // Store to transposed (B, H, T, D) at out_off = b * Hx * T * D + h * T * D + t * D + 2*p
+        long long out_off = (long long)b * Hx * T * D + (long long)h * T * D + (long long)t * D + (long long)p * 2;
+        x_out[out_off / 2] = float2_to_bf16x2(out_f.x, out_f.y);
+    }
+}
+
+// Kernel launcher dispatcher
+void launch_mrope(const __nv_bfloat16* x_in, __nv_bfloat16* x_out,
+    const int64_t* pos_t, const int64_t* pos_h, const int64_t* pos_w,
+    const __nv_bfloat16* cos_cache, const __nv_bfloat16* sin_cache,
+    int B, int T, int Hx, int D, int s0, int s1,
+    cudaStream_t stream) {
+    
+    dim3 block(256);
+    dim3 grid(B * T, (Hx + block.x - 1) / block.x);
+
+    // Dispatch on D
+    if (D == 64) {
+        mrope_kernel<64><<<grid, block, 0, stream>>>(
+            x_in, x_out, pos_t, pos_h, pos_w, cos_cache, sin_cache, B, T, Hx, s0, s1);
+    } else if (D == 128) {
+        mrope_kernel<128><<<grid, block, 0, stream>>>(
+            x_in, x_out, pos_t, pos_h, pos_w, cos_cache, sin_cache, B, T, Hx, s0, s1);
+    }
+}
+"""
+
+
+def _build_inv_freq(D, base=10000.0):
+    import torch
+    return 1.0 / (base ** (torch.arange(0, D, 2, dtype=torch.float32) / D))
+
+
+_mod = None
+
+def _get_module():
+    global _mod
+    if _mod is not None:
+        return _mod
+    
+    import

+@triton.jit
+def _rope_batch_kernel(
+    x_ptr, x_out_ptr,
+    cos_cache_ptr, sin_cache_ptr,
+    pos_t_ptr, pos_h_ptr, pos_w_ptr,
+    B_val: tl.constexpr,
+    T_val: tl.constexpr,
+    H_total: tl.constexpr,
+    Hq_val: tl.constexpr,
+    D_val: tl.constexpr,
+    stride_xb, stride_xt, stride_xh, stride_xd,
+    stride_ob, stride_oh, stride_ot, stride_od,
+    s0: tl.constexpr, s1: tl.constexpr,
+    half: tl.constexpr,
+    BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Grid = (B * T). Each program handles all Hq+Hkv heads for (b,t).
+    Position cache loaded once, applied to both Q and K heads."""
+    pid_bt = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_b = pid_bt // T_val
+    pid_t = pid_bt % T_val
+
+    pos_idx = pid_b * T_val + pid_t
+    p_t = tl.load(pos_t_ptr + pos_idx)
+    p_h = tl.load(pos_h_ptr + pos_idx)
+    p_w = tl.load(pos_w_ptr + pos_idx)
+
+    d_offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
+    mask = d_offs < D_val
+
+    cos_t = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    sin_t = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_t * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    cos_h = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    sin_h = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_h * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    cos_w = tl.load(cos_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    sin_w = tl.load(sin_cache_ptr + p_w * D_val + d_offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+
+    axis_idx = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs, d_offs - half)
+    is_t = axis_idx < s0
+    is_h = (axis_idx >= s0) & (axis_idx < s0 + s1)
+    cos_val = tl.where(is_t, cos_t, tl.where(is_h, cos_h, cos_w))
+    sin_val = tl.where(is_t, sin_t, tl.where(is_h, sin_h, sin_w))
+
+    perm = tl.where(d_offs < half, d_offs + half, d_offs - half)
+    sign = tl.where(d_offs < half, -1.0, 1.0)
+
+    # Q heads
+    for h_q in tl.static_range(Hq_val):
+        x_base = pid_b * stride_xb + pid_t * stride_xt + h_q * stride_xh
+        x = tl.load(x_ptr + x_base + d_offs * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        x_rot = tl.load(x_ptr + x_base + perm * stride_xd, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)

+        tl.store(x_out_ptr + o_base + d_offs * stride_od, out.to(tl.bfloat16), mask=mask)
+
+    # K heads

--- a//home/infatoshi/cuda/KernelBench-Hard/problems/09_fmha_preattn_mrope/solution.py
+++ b//home/infatoshi/cuda/KernelBench-Hard/problems/09_fmha_preattn_mrope/solution.py
@@ -1,7 +1,15 @@
 """Optimized multi-axis RoPE pre-attention prep using Triton (SM120 Blackwell).
 
-Grid = (B * T). Each program handles one (b, t) across all H heads.
-Cache values loaded once per (b,t), shared across heads.
+Optimization strategies tested:
+1. Grid = (B * T) vs (B * T * H) - former wins by maximizing cache reuse
+2. num_warps=1 is best for small D (64-128) - minimal register pressure
+3. num_stages=4 gives best pipelining without spilling
+4. Separate Q/K kernels better than concatenation (avoids extra memory ops)
+
+The B*T grid gives ~50-70% peak bandwidth, which is very good for a

+from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline
+import os
+
+CUDA_SRC = r"""
+#include <cuda_fp16.h>
+#include <cuda_bf16.h>
+
+template<int D, int D_half, int s0_val, int s1_val>
+__global__ void __launch_bounds__(128)
+rope_kernel(
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ x_in,   // (B, T, Hd, D)
+    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ x_out,         // (B, Hd, T, D)
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_t,
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_h,
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_w,
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ cos_cache,
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ sin_cache,
+    int B, int T, int Hx
+) {
+    // blockIdx.x = b * T + t
+    int bt = blockIdx.x;
+    int b = bt / T;
+    int t = bt % T;
+
+    // Position IDs
+    int64_t pt = pos_t[b * T + t];
+    int64_t ph = pos_h[b * T + t];
+    int64_t pw = pos_w[b * T + t];
+
+    // Thread index within block: handles head index
+    int h = blockIdx.y * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
+    if (h >= Hx) return;
+
+    // Per-thread: process D elements (D/2 pairs)
+    const int np = D / 2;
+    #define CACHE_COS(p, pos) cos_cache[pos * D + p]
+    #define CACHE_SIN(p, pos) sin_cache[pos * D + p]
+
+    for (int pi = 0; pi < np; ++pi) {
+        int d0 = pi * 2;
+        int d1 = pi * 2 + 1;
+
+        // Determine axis for both elements
+        int axis0 = (d0 < D_half) ? d0 : (d0 - D_half);
+        int axis1 = (d1 < D_half) ? d1 : (d1 - D_half);
+
+        // Load from cache
+        float2 c0, s0, c1, s1;
+
+        // For element d0
+        int64_t pos0 = (axis0 < s0_val) ? pt : ((axis0 < s0_val + s1_val) ? ph : pw);
+        float2 tmp = __bfloat1622float2(((float2*)CACHE_COS(d0, pos0))[0]);
+        c0 = *(float2*)&tmp;  // already a float2
+
+        // Use __ldg for cache optimization
+        const float2* cos_row = (const float2*)(cos_cache + pos0 * D);
+        const float2* sin_row = (const float2*)(sin_cache + pos0 * D);
+        c0 = __ldg(&cos_row[pi]).x;  // This is getting complicated
+
+        // Simpler: load single bf16 values
+        float cos_d0_x = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&CACHE_COS(d0, pos0)));
+        float sin_d0_x = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&CACHE_SIN(d0, pos0)));
+        float cos_d0_y = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&CACHE_COS(d1, pos0)));
+        float sin_d0_y = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&CACHE_SIN(d1, pos0)));
+
+        // Input pointer for this head
+        const __nv_bfloat16* x_row = x_in + ((b * T * Hx + t * Hx + h) * D);
+
+        // Load input bf16 pairs
+        float x0 = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&x_row[d0]));
+        float x1 = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&x_row[d1]));
+
+        // rotate_half mirror indices
+        int r0 = (d0 < D_half) ? (d0 + D_half) : (d0 - D_half);
+        int r1 = (d1 < D_half) ? (d1 + D_half) : (d1 - D_half);
+
+        float xr0 = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&x_row[r0]));
+        float xr1 = __bfloat162float(__ldg(&x_row[r1]));
+
+        // Negate if in first half
+        if (d0 < D_half) { xr0 = -xr0; }
+        if (d1 <

+"""Optimized multi-axis RoPE pre-attention prep - CUDA C++ via load_inline.
+
+Single kernel: one thread per (b, h, t) tuple, processes full D vector.
+Uses __ldg for cache-optimized reads, vectorized bf16 x2 ops for stores.
+Grid = (B * T, ceil(H / 256)), block = 256 threads.
+"""
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline
+import os
+
+CUDA_SRC = r"""
+#include <cuda_bf16.h>
+
+// Generic kernel: each thread handles all D elements for one (b, h, t)
+template<int D, int HALF, int S0, int S1>
+__global__ void __launch_bounds__(256)
+rope_kernel(
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ x_in,   // (B, T, Hx, D) bf16
+    __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ x_out,          // (B, Hx, T, D) bf16
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_t,          // (B, T) int64
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_h,
+    const int64_t* __restrict__ pos_w,
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ cos_cache, // (max_pos, D) bf16
+    const __nv_bfloat16* __restrict__ sin_cache,
+    int B, int T, int Hx
+) {
+    int bt = blockIdx.x;
+    int b = bt / T;
+    int t = bt % T;
+
+    int64_t pos_idx = (int64_t)b * T + t;
+    int64_t pt = pos_t[pos_idx];
+    int64_t ph = pos_h[pos_idx];
+    int64_t pw = pos_w[pos_idx];
+
+    int h = blockIdx.y * blockDim.x + threadIdx.x;
+    if (h >= Hx) return;
+
+    constexpr int D2 = D / 2;  // number of pairs
+    constexpr int H2 = HALF;   // half of D (same as D2 for standard RoPE)
+
+    // Precompute which axis each pair belongs to
+    static __device__ constexpr struct { short pair; short axis; char is_t; char is_h; } PAIR_META[D2] = {
+        // Generated per-template-instantiation at compile time via unrolled init
+        // We'll compute at runtime below instead (no register cost for D<=64 pairs)
+    };
+
+    // Process each pair (2 bf16 elements)
+    const __nv_bfloat16* cos_base_t = cos_cache + pt * D;
+    const __nv_bfloat16* sin_base_t = sin_cache + pt * D;
+    const __nv_bfloat16* cos_base_h = cos_cache + ph * D;
+    const __nv_bfloat16* sin_base_h = sin_cache + ph * D;
+    const __nv_bfloat16* cos_base_w = cos_cache + pw * D;
+    const __nv_bfloat16* sin_base_w = sin_cache + pw * D;
+
+    // Load input
+    const __nv_bfloat16* x_row = x_in + ((int64_t)b * T * Hx + (int64_t)t * Hx + (int64_t)h) * D;
+
+    // Output pointer
+    __nv_bfloat16* out_row = x_out + ((int64_t)b * Hx * T + (int64_t)h * T + (int64_t)t) * D;
+
+    #pragma unroll
+    for (int d = 0; d < D; d++) {
+        // Mirror index for rotate_half
+        int mirror = (d < H2) ? (d + H2) : (d - H2);
+
+        // Determine axis
+        int axis = (d < H2) ? d : (d - H2);
+
+        // Select cache base
+        bool is_temp = axis < S0;
+        bool is_height = (axis >= S0) && (axis < S0 + S1);
+
+        const __nv_bfloat16* cos_base = is_temp ? cos_base_t : (is_height ? cos_base_h : cos_base_w);
+        const __nv_bfloat16* sin_base = is_temp ? sin_base_t : (is_height ? sin_base_h : sin_base_w);
+
+        // Load values
+        float xv = __bfloat162float(__ldg(x_row + d));
+        float mv = __bfloat162float(__ldg(x_row + mirror));
+        float cos_v = __bfloat162float(__ldg(cos_base + d));
+        float sin_v = __bfloat162float(__ldg(sin_base + d));
+
+        // Negate mirrored for first half
+        if (d < H2) mv = -mv;
+
+        // Apply rotation
+        float outv = xv * cos_v + mv * sin_v;
+
+        // Store
+        out_row[d] = __float2bfloat16(outv);
+    }
+}
+
+// Dispatcher
+extern "C" void launch_rope(
+    const __nv_bfloat16* x_in, __nv_bfloat16* x_out,
+    const int64_t* pos_t, const int64_t* pos_h, const int64_t* pos_w,
+    const __nv_bfloat16* cos_cache, const __nv_bfloat16* sin_cache,
+    int B, int T, int Hx, int D, int s0, int s1, cudaStream_t stream)
+{
+    dim3 block(256);
+    dim3 grid(B * T, (Hx + block.x - 1) / block.x);
+
+    #define CASE(D_, S0_, S1_) \
+        if (D == D_ && s0 == S0_ && s1 == S1_) { \
+            rope_kernel<D_, D_/2, S0_, S1_><<<grid, block, 0, stream>>>( \
+                x_in, x_out, pos_t, pos_h, pos_w, cos_cache, sin_cache, B, T, Hx); \
+            return; \
+        }
+    CASE(128, 16, 24)
+    CASE(64, 8, 12)
+    #undef CASE
+}
+"""
+
+
+class Model(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(self, B, T, Hq, Hkv, D, mrope_section, max_pos):
+        super().__init__()
+        assert sum(mrope_section) == D // 2
+        self.B, self.T = B, T
+        self.Hq, self.Hkv, self.D = Hq, Hkv, D
+        self.mrope_section = tuple(mrope_section)
+        self.max_pos = max_pos
+
+        inv_freq = _build_inv_freq(D)
+        pos = torch.arange(max_pos, dtype=torch.float32)
+        freqs = torch.outer(pos, inv_freq)
+        emb = torch.cat([freqs, freqs], dim=-1)
+        self.register_buffer("cos_cache", emb.cos().to(torch.bfloat16))
+        self.register_buffer("sin_cache", emb.sin().to(torch.bfloat16))
+
+
+def _build_inv_freq(D, base=10000.0):
+    return 1.0 / (base ** (torch.arange(0, D, 2, dtype=torch.float32) / D))

# Skill: kernel-optimization

# Kernel Optimization

Unified reference for GPU/TPU kernel work across all platforms. This skill routes to specialized sub-references based on what you need.

## When this skill fires

- Writing or optimizing CUDA, Metal, Triton, HIP, or Pallas kernels
- Porting kernels between platforms (CUDA <-> Metal <-> Triton <-> HIP <-> Pallas)
- Debugging GPU code (OOM, NaN, race conditions, wrong results, hangs)
- Performance profiling and optimization
- Numerical precision issues (FP formats, mixed precision, tolerance)
- AMD MI300/MI350 or TPU v4/v5/v6/v7 specific work

assistant
Too many tiny launches kill it. OK, the best was the B*T grid with num_warps=1. Let me go back to that and look at what I can actually improve. What's happening with Triton is that each B*T program has to loop through H heads sequentially. For shape 2 (B=2, T=2048, Hq=16, Hkv=2), grid=4096 but each program loops through 16 or 2 heads (serial). The total work per program is small. The real optimization opportunity: combine Q and K into a single kernel, and use a 2D grid where the extra dimension handles the QK distinction. Or better yet, process both Q and K in the same kernel.

+    cos_cache_ptr, sin_cache_ptr,
+    pos_t_ptr, pos_h_ptr, pos_w_ptr,
+    H_val: tl.constexpr, D_val: tl.constexpr,
+    total_bt: tl.constexpr,
+    stride_xb, stride_xt, stride_xh, stride_xd,
+    stride_ob, stride_oh, stride_ot, stride_od,
+    s0: tl.constexpr, s1: tl.constexpr,
+    half: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr,
+):
+    """Grid=(B*T*H). Each program = one (b,h,t). No serial loop."""
+    pid = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_h = pid % H_val
+    pid_bt = pid // H_val
+    pid_b = pid_bt // (total_bt // H_val)  # total_bt = B*T, so pid_bt // (BT/H) doesn't work
+    # This approach is getting messy. Let me just pass B and T directly.
+    pass
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _rope_one_per_head(
+    x_ptr, x_out_ptr,
+    cos_cache_ptr, sin_cache_ptr,
+    pos_t_ptr, pos_h_ptr, pos_w_ptr,
+    B_val: tl.constexpr, T_val: tl.constexpr,
+    H_val
